REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.removeFlexInterstices = function () {
$('#panel_0').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass("intersticeOff");
$('#panel_1').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass("intersticeOff");
}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.clearRightPanel = function () {
$('#pricePanel').removeClass('intersticeOff').addClass ('intersticeOn');

$('#date1Right').html ('');
$('.outAdtPrice').html ("-");
$('.outChdPrice').html ("-");
$('.outYthPrice').html ("-");
$('.outStuPrice').html ("-");
$('.outInfPrice').html ("-");
$(".fareCurrency").html('');
$('.fareCurrencyOutbound').html('');

REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.manageBackButton = function () {
var lFareFamilyOut = WDSCommon.getTagValue( document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.OUTBOUND_FARE_FAMILY_CODE );
if (document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_1 ) {
if ( WDSCommon.getTagValue( document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_1 ) != '' ) {
this.preselectFlight = false;
var lFlightOut = WDSCommon.getTagValue( document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_1 );
var objOutbound = document.getElementById("reco_0_" + lFlightOut + "_" + lFareFamilyOut);
this.selectFlight(lFareFamilyOut,lFlightOut,0,objOutbound);
}
}

var lFareFamilyIn = WDSCommon.getTagValue(document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.INBOUND_FARE_FAMILY_CODE);
if (document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_2) {
if (WDSCommon.getTagValue(document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_2) != '') {
this.preselectFlight = false;
var lFlightIn = WDSCommon.getTagValue(document.REV_ADV_CO_FORM.FLIGHT_ID_2);
var objInbound = document.getElementById("reco_1_" + lFlightIn + "_" + lFareFamilyIn);
this.selectFlight(lFareFamilyIn, lFlightIn, 1, objInbound);
}
}


}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.updateRightPanel = function (date1, date2,
priceOutAdt, priceOutChd, priceOutInf, priceOutYth, priceOutStu,
priceInAdt, priceInChd, priceInInf, priceInYth, priceInStu,
points, currency, sfee, taxes, listTaxes, totalCash, totalPriceValue, trace, minPricePoint,
outboundPricePoint, inboundPricePoint, outboundBLocation, outboundELocation, inboundBLocation, inboundELocation,
fuelSurcharge, baseFare, totalAmount, totalConvertedCashMiles, fareBasis,
baseFareOutbound, baseFareInbound, taxOutbound, taxInbound,
basePerPax, taxPerPax, fuelPerPax, warningDifferentAirport,mode,error8015,warningChangeOfAirport){
WDSError.removeAllWarning();
WDSError.removeError("Please select a return flight");
WDSError.removeError("Please select an outward flight");
WDSError.showIfErrorOrWarning();
$('#date1Right').html (date1);
$('#date2Right').html (date2);
$('#b_location_1').html (outboundBLocation);
$('#e_location_1').html (outboundELocation);
$('#b_location_2').html (inboundBLocation);
$('#e_location_2').html (inboundELocation);
if (priceOutAdt != null)
$('.outAdtPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutAdt)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutYth != null)
$('.outYthPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutYth)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutStu != null)
$('.outStuPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutStu)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutChd != null) {
$('.outChdPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutChd)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
if (priceOutInf != null) {
$('.outInfPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutInf)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
$('.fareCurrencyOutbound').html(currency);

if (priceInAdt != null)
$('.inAdtPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInAdt)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInYth != null)
$('.inYthPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInYth)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInStu != null)
$('.inStuPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInStu)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInChd != null) {
$('.inChdPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInChd)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
if (priceInInf != null) {
$('.inInfPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInInf)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
$('.fareCurrencyInbound').html(currency);

$('#fareRuleOutboundCluster').css("display", "inline");
$('#fareRuleInboundCluster').css("display", "inline");
/*$('#totalPoints').html(parseFloat(points)).format(theCommonFunctions.pointsPattern);
$('#totalPointsToBeUsed').html(parseFloat(points)).format(theCommonFunctions.pointsPattern);
this.totalPoints = points;*/
$('#debug').html(trace);
$('.fareCurrency').html(currency);
/*$('#minimumPoints').html (minPricePoint);
$('#outboundPointPrice').html (outboundPricePoint);
$('#inboundPointPrice').html (inboundPricePoint);*/

$('#totalPriceCash').html (parseFloat(totalCash)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (sfee!='null' && sfee!=0)
{
$('#displayFees').css("display", "block");
$('#ServiceFee').html (parseFloat(sfee)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
$('#currencySFee').html (currency);
}
else $('#displayFees').css("display", "none");
if (taxes!=0)
{
$('#displayBreakdownTaxes').css("display", "block");
}
else {
$('#displayBreakdownTaxes').css("display", "none");
}

if(mode == "TAXBREAKDOWN"  || mode =="FARERULE"){
theCommonFunctions.populateToolTip("Breakdown of taxes and &lt;br&gt;carrier-imposed fees",'rightPanelTaxesToolTip',listTaxes);
this.taxBreakdownHtml = listTaxes;
$('#contentToolTip').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass ("intersticeOff");
if(error8015){$('#WDSPoptip').css("top","350px");}
}
$('#taxesAndFees').html (parseFloat(taxes)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
$('#currencyTaxesAndFees').html (currency);
$('#currencyTotalPriceCash').html (currency);
if (warningDifferentAirport){
WDSError.addWarning("Note: Arrival airport is different on your return flight.");
WDSError.show();
}
if (warningChangeOfAirport){
WDSError.addWarning("Airport change in itinerary");
WDSError.show();
}
if(typeof DiscrepancyDataObj != 'undefined'){
DiscrepancyDataObj.showDiscrepancyWarning();
}
/* Update the Slider
slider.init(



null


,
theREV_AVD_ODForm.currentPoints, parseInt(minPricePoint),outboundPricePoint, inboundPricePoint, currency, totalPriceValue);*/
}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.getFareAfterBackFromFPS = function (boundId) {

}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.getFare = function (mode) {
if(mode == "NEXTACTION" && (this.flightId1 == ''|| this.flightId2 == '') ){
this.check();
if (WDSError.hasError()) {
WDSError.show();
}
}
this.lastFareCallRecoId1 = this.recoId1;
this.lastFareCallRecoId2 = this.recoId2;
if (this.flightId1 != ''&& this.flightId2 != '') {
myDialog.open();
this.clearRightPanel();
var dataForRq = {
"format" : "json",
"error" : "json",
"SITE": "SKBKSKBK",
"TRIP_TYPE": "R",
"LANGUAGE":"GB",
"PAGE_TICKET": "0",
"FLIGHT_ID_1": this.flightId1,
"OUTBOUND_FARE_FAMILY_CODE": this.currentOutboundFare,
"RECO_ID_1": this.recoId1,
"PREV_RECO_ID_1":this.lastFareCallRecoId1,
"RECOMMENDATION_ID_1": this.recoId1
,
"RECO_ID_2": this.recoId2,
"FLIGHT_ID_2": this.flightId2,
"INBOUND_FARE_FAMILY_CODE": this.currentInboundFare,
"RECOMMENDATION_ID_2": this.recoId2,
"PREV_RECO_ID_2":this.lastFareCallRecoId2,

};
var idOutBound='toggleId_0_' + this.flightId1;
var idInBound='toggleId_1_' + this.flightId2;
var isViaInItinerary=false;
if ($('#' + idOutBound +' .stepOver').size() > 0 || $('#' + idInBound +' .stepOver').size() > 0 )
{
isViaInItinerary=true;
}


var fareUrl="";
if (!isViaInItinerary)
fareUrl="Fare.action?TAB_ID=TRNEJjwIqWKXAqyReSG7EToLhTQGsVLYc-Yp3GbWaSDXPLTrkttB!-1974264916!-1634085990!1547492212110";
else
fareUrl="Override.action?TAB_ID=TRNEJjwIqWKXAqyReSG7EToLhTQGsVLYc-Yp3GbWaSDXPLTrkttB!-1974264916!-1634085990!1547492212110";
if (isViaInItinerary)
{
dataForRq["EMBEDDED_TRANSACTION"] = "Fare";
dataForRq["SO_SITE_SHOW_STOP_CITIES"] = "TRUE";
}

if(!this.isFirstFaringDone){
dataForRq["GET_LOWEST_FARE"] = "TRUE";
this.isFirstFaringDone = true;
}

if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_ADULT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["price"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_ADULT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["tax"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_ADULT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_CHILD_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["price"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_CHILD_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["tax"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_CHILD_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_YOUTH_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["price"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_YOUTH_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["tax"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_YOUTH_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_STUDENT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["price"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_STUDENT_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["tax"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_STUDENT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_INFANT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["price"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_INFANT_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["tax"];
dataForRq["OUTBOUND_INFANT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}

if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["INBOUND_ADULT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["price"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_ADULT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["tax"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_ADULT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["INBOUND_CHILD_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["price"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_CHILD_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["tax"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_CHILD_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["INBOUND_YOUTH_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["price"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_YOUTH_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["tax"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_YOUTH_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["INBOUND_STUDENT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["price"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_STUDENT_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["tax"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_STUDENT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["price"] != "undefined"){
dataForRq["INBOUND_INFANT_PRICE"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["price"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_INFANT_TAX"] =  this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["tax"];
dataForRq["INBOUND_INFANT_PRICE_WITHOUT_TAX"] = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["priceWithoutTax"];
}

$.jsonp({
url: fareUrl,
data: dataForRq,
dataType: "jsonp",
callbackParameter: "jsoncallback",
success: function(data, status){
$.each(data.result, function(i,item){
if (item.code=='ko') {
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
WDSError.add (item.text);
WDSError.show();
theREV_AVD_COForm.resubmitAVD = true;
theREV_AVD_COForm.errorInFare = true;
theREV_AVD_COForm.eraseShoppingBasket();
$('#pricePanel').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass ("intersticeOff");
theCommonFunctions.desactivateFQN();
}else{
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "FLIGHT_ID_1", item.flight1);
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "OUTBOUND_FARE_FAMILY_CODE", item.outboundff);
if(item.error8015){
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
WDSError.add (item.text);
WDSError.show();
}
else if (!item.error8015){
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
}
theREV_AVD_COForm.updateRightPanel(
item.date1fmt, item.date2fmt,
item.priceOutAdt, item.priceOutChd,item.priceOutInf, item.priceOutYth, item.priceOutStu,
item.priceInAdt, item.priceInChd,item.priceInInf, item.priceInYth, item.priceInStu,
parseFloat(item.pointsToPay, 10), item.currency, parseFloat(item.fee, 10), parseFloat(item.tax, 10),
item.listTaxes, item.totalPrice, item.totalPriceValue,
item.trace, parseFloat(item.minPricePoint, 10),
parseFloat(item.outboundPricePoint, 10), parseFloat(item.inboundPricePoint, 10),
item.outboundBLocation, item.outboundELocation,
item.inboundBLocation, item.inboundELocation,
parseFloat(item.fuelSurcharge, 10), parseFloat(item.baseFare, 10),
item.totalAmount, parseFloat(item.totalConvertedCashMiles, 10), item.fareBasis,
parseFloat(item.baseFareOutbound, 10), parseFloat(item.baseFareInbound, 10),
parseFloat(item.taxOutbound, 10), parseFloat(item.taxInbound, 10),
parseFloat(item.basePerPax, 10),parseFloat(item.taxPerPax, 10), parseFloat(item.fuelPerPax, 10), item.warningDifferentAirport, mode,item.error8015,item.warningChangeOfAirport);


var sSasCreditsRange='2-6';
var aSasCreditsRange=sSasCreditsRange.split('-');
if (aSasCreditsRange.length==2)
{
var iSasCreditsRangeLow=parseInt(aSasCreditsRange[0],10);
var iSasCreditsRangeHigh=parseInt(aSasCreditsRange[1],10);
var sValueRangeLow=item.totalPrice * iSasCreditsRangeLow / 100;
var sValueRangeHigh=item.totalPrice * iSasCreditsRangeHigh / 100;
$('#sasCredits').css("display","block");
$('#sasCreditRangeLow').html(Math.round(sValueRangeLow));
$('#sasCreditRangeHigh').html(Math.round(sValueRangeHigh));
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "MIN_CREDIT_POINTS", Math.round(sValueRangeLow));
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "MAX_CREDIT_POINTS", Math.round(sValueRangeHigh));
}



var computedTotal = null;
var nbChild = 0;
var nbInfant = 0;
var nbAdult = 1;


computedTotal = nbAdult*item.priceOutAdt;
computedTotal += nbAdult*item.priceInAdt;
if(nbChild > 0){
computedTotal += nbChild*item.priceOutChd;
computedTotal += nbChild*item.priceInChd;
}
if(nbInfant > 0){
computedTotal += nbInfant*item.priceOutInf;
computedTotal += nbInfant*item.priceInInf;
}
computedTotal += parseFloat(item.fee, 10);


theREV_AVD_COForm.updateFaresInPricePanel(item.outboundff,item.inboundff);
theREV_AVD_COForm.pageTicket = item.pageTicket;
theREV_AVD_COForm.resubmitAVD = false;


$('#pricePanel').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass ("intersticeOff");
WDSCommon.updateTag (document.REV_AVD_CO_FORM, "CABIN", item.cabin);
WDSCommon.updateTag (document.NEWDATE_FORM, "PAGE_TICKET", item.pageTicket);
theCommonFunctions.activateFQN();
if(mode == "NEXTACTION" ){
theREV_AVD_COForm.submit();
}
if(mode == "PREVIOUSDAY" || mode == "SWITCHTAB" || mode == "NEXTDAY"){
theNEWDATEForm.submitFromCalendar();
}
}
myDialog.close();
});
},
error: function(XHR, textStatus, errorThrown){
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
WDSError.add(WDSMessage.getMessage("REV_AVD_CO.js.TimeoutFareError"));
WDSError.show();
$('#pricePanel').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass ("intersticeOff");
theREV_AVD_COForm.resubmitAVD = true;
theREV_AVD_COForm.errorInFare = true;
theREV_AVD_COForm.eraseShoppingBasket();
myDialog.close();
}
})
}
}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.check = function () {
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
if ( !this.resubmitAVD ) {


if (this.flightId1 == '') {
WDSError.add(WDSMessage.getMessage("REV_AVD_CO.js.SelectYourDepartureFlight"));
myDialog.close();
}
if (this.flightId2 == '') {
WDSError.add(WDSMessage.getMessage("REV_AVD_CO.js.SelectYourArrivalFlight"));
myDialog.close();
}



}
}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.eraseShoppingBasket = function (){
if (this.resubmitAVD) {
this.resubmitAVD = false;
if (this.errorInFare) {
$('#toggleId_0'+'_'+theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId1).stop(true, true);
$('#toggleId_0'+'_'+theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId1).css("display", "none");
theCommonFunctions.unselectEffect ("reco_0" + "_" + theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId1 + "_" + theREV_AVD_COForm.currentOutboundFare);
$('#toggleId_1'+'_'+theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId2).stop(true, true);
$('#toggleId_1'+'_'+theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId2).css("display", "none");
theCommonFunctions.unselectEffect ("reco_1" + "_" + theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId2 + "_" + theREV_AVD_COForm.currentInboundFare);
}
this.flightId1 = '';
this.recoId1 = '';
this.flightId2 = '';
this.recoId2 = '';
this.clearRightPanel();







this.updateDatesInPricePanel ('Mon 4 Feb 2019', 'Sun 10 Feb 2019');
}
}

REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.updateFlexPricerRightPanel = function (date1, date2,
priceOutAdt, priceOutChd,priceOutYth, priceOutStu,priceOutInf,
priceInAdt, priceInChd,priceInYth, priceInStu,priceInInf,
currency, sfee, taxes,totalCash,outboundBLocation, outboundELocation, inboundBLocation, inboundELocation,
warningDifferentAirport){
WDSError.removeAllWarning();
WDSError.removeError("Please select a return flight");
WDSError.removeError("Please select an outward flight");
WDSError.showIfErrorOrWarning();
$('#date1Right').html (date1);
$('#date2Right').html (date2);
$('#b_location_1').html (outboundBLocation);
$('#e_location_1').html (outboundELocation);
$('#b_location_2').html (inboundBLocation);
$('#e_location_2').html (inboundELocation);
if (priceOutAdt != null)
$('.outAdtPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutAdt)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutYth != null)
$('.outYthPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutYth)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutStu != null)
$('.outStuPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutStu)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceOutChd != null) {
$('.outChdPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutChd)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
if (priceOutInf != null) {
$('.outInfPrice').html(parseFloat(priceOutInf)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
$('.fareCurrencyOutbound').html(currency);

if (priceInAdt != null)
$('.inAdtPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInAdt)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInYth != null)
$('.inYthPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInYth)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInStu != null)
$('.inStuPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInStu)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (priceInChd != null) {
$('.inChdPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInChd)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
if (priceInInf != null) {
$('.inInfPrice').html(parseFloat(priceInInf)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
}
$('.fareCurrencyInbound').html(currency);

$('#fareRuleOutboundCluster').css("display", "inline");
$('#fareRuleInboundCluster').css("display", "inline");

$('#taxesPopIn').click(function(){
theREV_AVD_COForm.updateTaxBreakdown();
});
$('.fareCurrency').html(currency);
$('#totalPriceCash').html (parseFloat(totalCash)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
if (sfee!='null' && sfee!=0)
{
$('#displayFees').css("display", "block");
$('#ServiceFee').html (parseFloat(sfee)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
$('#currencySFee').html (currency);
}
else $('#displayFees').css("display", "none");
if (taxes!=0)
{
$('#displayBreakdownTaxes').css("display", "block");
}
else {
$('#displayBreakdownTaxes').css("display", "none");
}
$('#taxesAndFees').html (parseFloat(taxes)).format(theCommonFunctions.priceTwoDecimalsPattern);
$('#currencyTaxesAndFees').html (currency);
$('#currencyTotalPriceCash').html (currency);
if (warningDifferentAirport){
WDSError.addWarning("Note: Arrival airport is different on your return flight.");
WDSError.show();
}
if(typeof DiscrepancyDataObj != 'undefined'){
DiscrepancyDataObj.showDiscrepancyWarning();
}
}
REV_AVD_COForm.prototype.getFlexPricerFare = function(){
if (this.flightId1 != ''&& this.flightId2 != '') {
myDialog.open();
WDSError.init();
WDSError.reset();
this.clearRightPanel();
var warningDifferentAirport,date1fmt,flight1,outboundff,outboundBLocation,outboundELocation;
var date2fmt,flight2,inboundff,inboundBLocation,inboundELocation;
var currency,listTaxes,priceOutAdt,priceInAdt,priceOutChd,priceInChd,priceOutYth,priceInYth,priceOutStu,priceInStu,priceOutInf,priceInInf;



date1fmt ='Mon 4 Feb 2019';
outboundBLocation ='Stockholm (ARN)';
outboundELocation ='London (LHR)';
outboundff = this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["fareFamily"];




date2fmt ='Sun 10 Feb 2019';
inboundBLocation ='London (LHR)';
inboundELocation ='Stockholm (ARN)';
inboundff  = this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["fareFamily"];

var price ="priceWithoutTax";

price ="price";

var tax= 0,fee = 0,totalPrice = 0,nbChild = 0,nbInfant = 0,nbYth = 0,nbStu = 0;
var nbAdult = 1;




if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceOutAdt = parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["ADT"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceOutAdt*nbAdult;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceOutChd = parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["CHD"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceOutChd*nbChild;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceOutYth = parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["YTH"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceOutYth*nbYth;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceOutStu = parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["STU"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceOutStu*nbStu;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceOutInf = parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsOutbound[this.recoId1]["INF"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceOutInf*nbInfant;
}

if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceInAdt = parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["ADT"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceInAdt*nbAdult;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceInChd = parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["CHD"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceInChd*nbChild;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceInYth = parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["YTH"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceInYth*nbYth;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceInStu = parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["STU"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceInStu*nbStu;
}
if(typeof this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["price"] != "undefined"){
priceInInf = parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"][price]);
tax= tax + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["tax"]);
fee = fee + parseFloat(this.recommendationsInbound[this.recoId2]["INF"]["fee"]);
totalPrice = 	totalPrice + priceInInf*nbInfant;
}

currency = 'EUR';
totalPrice = totalPrice+ tax+fee;

totalPrice =totalPrice - tax;

theREV_AVD_COForm.updateFlexPricerRightPanel(date1fmt,date2fmt,priceOutAdt,priceOutChd,priceOutYth,priceOutStu,priceOutInf,priceInAdt,priceInChd,priceInYth,priceInStu,priceInInf,currency,fee,tax,totalPrice,outboundBLocation,outboundELocation,inboundBLocation,inboundELocation);


var sSasCreditsRange='2-6';
var aSasCreditsRange=sSasCreditsRange.split('-');
if (aSasCreditsRange.length==2)
{
var iSasCreditsRangeLow=parseInt(aSasCreditsRange[0],10);
var iSasCreditsRangeHigh=parseInt(aSasCreditsRange[1],10);
var sValueRangeLow=totalPrice * iSasCreditsRangeLow / 100;
var sValueRangeHigh=totalPrice * iSasCreditsRangeHigh / 100;
$('#sasCredits').css("display","block");
$('#sasCreditRangeLow').html(Math.round(sValueRangeLow));
$('#sasCreditRangeHigh').html(Math.round(sValueRangeHigh));
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "MIN_CREDIT_POINTS", Math.round(sValueRangeLow));
WDSCommon.updateTag (theREV_AVD_COForm.getForm(), "MAX_CREDIT_POINTS", Math.round(sValueRangeHigh));
}

theREV_AVD_COForm.updateFaresInPricePanel(outboundff,inboundff);
theREV_AVD_COForm.resubmitAVD = false;
$('#pricePanel').removeClass("intersticeOn").addClass ("intersticeOff");
theCommonFunctions.activateFQN();
myDialog.close();
}
}

}

}

this.getFare("TAXBREAKDOWN");}
else{

theCommonFunctions.populateToolTip('Breakdown of taxes and &lt;br&gt;carrier-imposed fees','rightPanelTaxesToolTip',theREV_AVD_COForm.taxBreakdownHtml);
}
};
/**
* Change the time window filter.
*/
NEWDATEForm.prototype.changeTimeWindowFilter = function (){
myDialog.open();
var mode1 = $("#timeWindow_0").val();
var date1 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_DATE_1]');
var anyTime1 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_ANY_TIME_1]');
var bTimeWindow1 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_TIME_WINDOW_1]');
if (anyTime1.length == 0){
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM]').append( $('<input type="hidden" name="B_ANY_TIME_1" />') );
anyTime1 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_ANY_TIME_1]');
}
if (bTimeWindow1.length == 0){
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM]').append( $('<input type="hidden" name="B_TIME_WINDOW_1" value="3" />') );
}
if (mode1 == "ALL_DAY"){
date1.val(date1.val().substring(0,8) + "0000");
anyTime1.val("TRUE");
}
if (mode1 == "MORNING"){
date1.val(date1.val().substring(0,8) + "0900");
anyTime1.val("FALSE");
}
if (mode1 == "AFTERNOON"){
date1.val(date1.val().substring(0,8) + "1500");
anyTime1.val("FALSE");
}
if (mode1 == "EVENING"){
date1.val(date1.val().substring(0,8) + "2100");
anyTime1.val("FALSE");
}
if ($("#timeWindow_1").length != 0){
var mode2 = $("#timeWindow_1").val();
var date2 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_DATE_2]');
var anyTime2 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_ANY_TIME_2]');
var bTimeWindow2 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_TIME_WINDOW_2]');
if (anyTime2.length == 0){
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM]').append( $('<input type="hidden" name="B_ANY_TIME_2" />') );
anyTime2 = $('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=B_ANY_TIME_2]');
}
if (bTimeWindow2.length == 0){
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM]').append( $('<input type="hidden" name="B_TIME_WINDOW_2" value="3" />') );
}
if (mode2 == "ALL_DAY"){
date2.val(date2.val().substring(0,8) + "0000");
anyTime2.val("TRUE");
}
if (mode2 == "MORNING"){
date2.val(date2.val().substring(0,8) + "0900");
anyTime2.val("FALSE");
}
if (mode2 == "AFTERNOON"){
date2.val(date2.val().substring(0,8) + "1500");
anyTime2.val("FALSE");
}
if (mode2 == "EVENING"){
date2.val(date2.val().substring(0,8) + "2100");
anyTime2.val("FALSE");
}
this.checkTimeWindow(date1, date2);
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=WDS_KEEP_TABS_2]').val('true');
}
$('form[name=NEWDATE_FORM] :input[name=WDS_KEEP_TABS_1]').val('true');
NEWDATEForm.superclass.submit.call(this);
}
NEWDATEForm.prototype.checkTimeWindow = function (date1, date2) {
if (date1.val() == "" || date2.val() == "" || date1.val().substring(0,8) != date2.val().substring(0,8)){
return;
}
var hour1 = parseInt(date1.val().substring(8,10), 10);
var hour2 = parseInt(date2.val().substring(8,10), 10);
if (hour1 > hour2){
if (hour2 == 0){
date2.val(date2.val().substring(0,8) + "2300");
}else{
date2.val(date1.val());
}
}
}
NEWDATEForm.prototype.submitFromCalendar = function(){
NEWDATEForm.superclass.submit.call(this);
}
NEWDATEForm.prototype.submit = function (prevOrNext, flight, nbDays){
myDialog.open();
dateToChange = "B_DATE_"+flight;
theREV_AVD_COForm.shoppingBasket = true;
var outboundFlightId = $("#panel_0 .priceSelectedEffectOff").attr("id");
if(typeof outboundFlightId == 'undefined'){
theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId1 = '';
}

var inboundFlightId = $("#panel_1 .priceSelectedEffectOff").attr("id");
if(typeof inboundFlightId == 'undefined'){
theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId2 = '';
}

if(prevOrNext == this.SWITCHTAB){
newDate = nbDays;
WDSCommon.updateTag(this.getForm(), 'WDS_KEEP_TABS_'+flight, 'true');
}
else {



WDSCommon.updateTag(this.getForm(), "ORIGINAL_B_DATE_"+flight, '');


varDate1 = WDSCommon.getTagValue(this.getForm(), dateToChange);
varAnnee = parseInt(varDate1.substring(0,4), 10);
varMois  = parseInt(varDate1.substring(4,6), 10)-1;
varJour  = parseInt(varDate1.substring(6,8), 10);
newDate1 = new Date(varAnnee, varMois, varJour,0,0,0);
if (prevOrNext==this.NEXTDAY) {
newDate1.setTime( newDate1.getTime() + ( 86400000 * nbDays ) - (newDate1.getTimezoneOffset()*60*1000));
} else {
newDate1.setTime( newDate1.getTime() - ( 86400000 * nbDays ) );
}
newDate = newDate1.getFullYear().toString(10);
if (newDate1.getMonth()<9) newDate += "0";
newDate += (newDate1.getMonth()+1).toString(10);
if (newDate1.getDate()<=9) newDate += "0";
newDate += newDate1.getDate().toString(10);
newDate += "0000";
WDSCommon.updateTag(this.getForm(), "ORIGINAL_B_DATE_"+flight, newDate);
}
WDSCommon.updateTag(this.getForm(), "B_DATE_"+flight, newDate);
bDate1 = WDSCommon.getTagValue(this.getForm(), 'B_DATE_1');
bDate2 = WDSCommon.getTagValue(this.getForm(), 'B_DATE_2');
if (bDate1 > bDate2) {
if(flight == '1'){
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'B_DATE_2', bDate1);
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'ORIGINAL_B_DATE_2', bDate1);
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'WDS_KEEP_TABS_2', '');
}else{
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'B_DATE_1', bDate2);
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'ORIGINAL_B_DATE_1', bDate2);
WDSCommon.updateTag (this.getForm(), 'WDS_KEEP_TABS_1', '');
}
}
if(theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId1 != ''&& theREV_AVD_COForm.flightId2 != ''){
theREV_AVD_COForm.getFare(prevOrNext);
}
else{
NEWDATEForm.superclass.submit.call(this);
}
}

}

BAPForm.prototype.getNewUserPoints = function () {
var form = this;
$.jsonp({

}
